name:Gâ€uâ€eâ€sâ€tâ€ â€Uâ€sâ€eâ€r
info:Business Garden-view Twin Room
info:Stayed in March 2024
info:Family
info:1 Review
rating:5
posted:Posted March 25, 2024
msg:I came to participate in the Jiujiang 2024 Marathon. After screening online, I booked the Peninsula Hotel near the event.
As soon as the car entered the hotel, I liked it because it was built on the mountain, lived by the water, and was scattered and open and quiet.
When checking in, Zhang Ying, the customer service at the front desk, received me skillfully and warmly (with free breakfast). The hotel is thoughtful as a whole, delaying the check-out time for the participants, and providing participants with free medical supplies in the lobby, such as Yunnan Baiyao, Qufeng Oil, Dianfu Stick, Band-Aids, etc.
The style of the buffet restaurant is simple and artistic. The pencil tower, lake, flowers and trees outside the window complement each other. The restaurant breakfast is a fusion of Chinese, Western and local snacks.
After checking out and leaving Jiujiang, I found that I had left two data cables the next day. After communicating with the service desk by phone, I found the lost items (at this point, I hope that the service can find the lost items of the last guest before the second guest checks in on the same day and inform them in time, instead of waiting for the guests to find them). Thanks to Shi Diying at the service desk for immediately delivering them to us by SF Express.
The overall experience is comfortable, pleasant and warm.
